## Next-finalization pointer (WI-2026-064)

The E1 open question (under [Execution Lifecycle Supervisor](#execution-lifecycle-supervisor)) is now **Resolved** by work item `074126de-11ed-437e-8327-495d2ee4b665` (WI-2026-064, short title: "Add test-driven override hook for ExecutionDispatchService.resolveIpFromOrchestrator (closes OPEN_QUESTIONS E1)"). The next finalization pass that touches this document should:

1. Reflect the E1 resolution in the per-pass `R#` entries (the resolution is independent of any specific pass, so it is recorded as a global pointer here rather than folded into a specific R# row).
2. Continue to enforce the legacy R25/R30 escalation sequence for the remaining E2–E9 questions (checkpoint deps consumers, paused/resumed consumers, frozen mid-sweep re-check, persistence recovery path coverage, projector subscription gap, subagent liveness probe spec gap, repository applyTransition patch-passthrough, version column passive). E2–E9 are not affected by WI-2026-064.
3. Continue to enforce the R25/R30 escalation sequence for the 5 still-failed split-retries (`oauth-auth-provider`, `oauth-login-service`, `cost-governance-runtime`, `war-room-lifecycle`, `war-room-collaboration`) and the 31st-pass followup questions (R105, R106, R107, R108, R111) until each is closed by a downstream work item.
4. Optionally re-probe the execution-lifecycle-supervisor scope if a structural change is detected in `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/` (the files added/touched by WI-2026-064); otherwise treat the `execution-lifecycle-supervisor` probe artifact as the canonical record of the resolved state.

The full implementation evidence is in:

- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-dispatch.service.types.ts` — new `IOrchestratorIpResolver` interface, `ORCHESTRATOR_IP_RESOLVER` DI token, four per-strategy DI tokens (`DEFAULT_ORCHESTRATOR_IP_RESOLVER`, `DNS_ROUND_ROBIN_IP_RESOLVER`, `SERVICE_MESH_HEADER_IP_RESOLVER`, `CUSTOM_HTTP_ENDPOINT_IP_RESOLVER`), and typed `OrchestratorIpResolutionError` for strategy-aware failure surfacing.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/default-orchestrator-ip-resolver.ts` — `default` strategy; parses the orchestrator URL via the WHATWG URL parser and returns its hostname. Stateless.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/dns-round-robin-ip-resolver.ts` — `dns_round_robin` strategy; A/AAAA lookup via `dns/promises.lookup` with 60s sticky cache per host, unbiased shuffle via `crypto.randomInt`, IPv6 bracket stripping before the DNS call.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/service-mesh-header-ip-resolver.ts` — `service_mesh_header` strategy; sentinel `GET /healthz` via `ContainerHttpClientService.httpGetRaw`, trusts the `X-Orchestrator-Ip` response header, validates against a full-form IPv4 / canonical IPv6 regex.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/custom-http-endpoint-ip-resolver.ts` — `custom_http_endpoint` strategy; reads `execution_dispatch_ip_resolver_endpoint` via `SystemSettingsService`, GETs the configured URL via `ContainerHttpClientService.httpGetRaw`, parses a `{ "ip": "..." }` JSON envelope, validates the IP literal.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/system-setting-orchestrator-ip-resolver.ts` — system-setting-based delegating resolver; reads `execution_dispatch_ip_resolver_override` on every call, validates via `isKnownResolverStrategy`, dispatches via exhaustive strategy switch, emits `ipResolved` / `ipResolutionFailed` telemetry, sanitizes the orchestrator URL (no userinfo / query / fragment in event payloads) and re-throws underlying resolver errors so the dispatch polling loop preserves its pre-Milestone-3 retry semantics. Also exports the `sanitizeOrchestratorUrl` helper used by tests.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-dispatch.settings.ts` — setting-key constants (`EXECUTION_DISPATCH_IP_RESOLVER_OVERRIDE_SETTING`, `EXECUTION_DISPATCH_IP_RESOLVER_ENDPOINT_SETTING`), event-name constants (`EXECUTION_DISPATCH_IP_RESOLVED_EVENT`, `EXECUTION_DISPATCH_IP_RESOLUTION_FAILED_EVENT`), `DEFAULT_RESOLVER_STRATEGY`, and the `isKnownResolverStrategy` type guard.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-event.publisher.ts` — `ipResolved` / `ipResolutionFailed` event publishers; aggregate identity is `'execution_dispatch'` (distinct from `'execution'`) with `aggregateId = orchestrator host` so outbox consumers can isolate the resolution stream.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-lifecycle.module.ts` — DI wiring for all four per-strategy tokens and the `ORCHESTRATOR_IP_RESOLVER` token (bound to `SystemSettingOrchestratorIpResolver` via `useClass`).
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-dispatch.service.ts` — consumer; replaced the legacy `protected resolveIpFromOrchestrator()` inline parser with `await this.ipResolver.resolve(orchestratorUrl)` against the injected `ORCHESTRATOR_IP_RESOLVER` token. The orchestrator URL is sourced from `process.env.ORCHESTRATOR_URL`; failures are logged + swallowed to `undefined` so the polling loop in `resolveContainerIp` retries.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/execution-dispatch.service.spec.ts` — updated to drop the legacy `TestableExecutionDispatchService` subclass and inject the resolver as `IOrchestratorIpResolver` directly in the test factory.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/default-orchestrator-ip-resolver.spec.ts` — 6 unit tests covering http/https/IPv4/URL-with-path scenarios and WHATWG parse failures.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/dns-round-robin-ip-resolver.spec.ts` — 8 unit tests with `vi.mock('node:dns/promises')` covering single-record, multi-record shuffle, sticky cache across calls, no-records error, DNS-layer error wrapping, IPv6 bracket stripping, and the optional `SystemSettingsService` constructor signature.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/service-mesh-header-ip-resolver.spec.ts` — 11 unit tests covering header success, IPv6 bracket stripping + shorthand rejection, whitespace trimming, array-valued header, missing header, invalid IP literal, non-200 status, HTTP-layer error wrapping (timeout), 2s timeout configuration, and the optional `SystemSettingsService` constructor signature.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/custom-http-endpoint-ip-resolver.spec.ts` — 14 unit tests covering the happy path, IPv6 bracket stripping + shorthand rejection, missing setting, empty/whitespace setting, malformed-URL setting, invalid JSON, missing `ip` field, empty `ip` field, invalid IP literal, non-200 status, ECONNREFUSED error wrapping, long-body truncation, and 2s timeout configuration.
- `apps/api/src/execution-lifecycle/system-setting-orchestrator-ip-resolver.spec.ts` — 17 unit tests covering strategy dispatch per override (all four strategies), fallback behavior (unknown value, unset, settings-service throws), failure telemetry with the strategy that actually ran, URL sanitization across both `ipResolved` and `ipResolutionFailed` events, malformed-URL passthrough in the sanitize helper, query / fragment stripping, and the static `token` accessor + per-strategy token identities.
- `docs/architecture/execution-lifecycle-supervisor.md` — new architecture doc covering the dispatch surface + §2 "Orchestrator IP Resolution Override (WI-2026-064)" with the DI token, the four strategies, the two setting keys, the two telemetry events, and the URL sanitization guarantee.
- `docs/architecture/README.md` — adds a link to the new `execution-lifecycle-supervisor.md` doc under "Runtime and Execution".
- This file (`docs/project-context/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`) — E1 marked Resolved by WI-2026-064.

No new open questions are introduced by this resolution.
